1932.07.06

Luo Tian County Magistrate Arrested Upon Arrival in the Province 1

(Hankou) Fang Dianjia, the magistrate of Luotian County, was arrested by the Civil Affairs Department upon his unauthorized arrival in the province after the county seat fell to bandits. He awaits instructions from Chiang Kai-shek. (5th dispatch)

Bandits Attacking Guangshui Repelled 2

(Beiping) According to sources in transportation circles, over two hundred bandits entrenched in Tianbingjian, Pingkang, Qin, and other areas, attacked Guangshui along Nanxin Store, attempting to cut off the Pinghan Railway again. They were met and defeated by government troops, who killed over a hundred bandits, with the rest fleeing. Traces of bandits have been frequently sighted near Guangshui, Donghuang Store, Yangjia Village, Wangjia Village, and other stations in recent days. Government troops are making efforts to search and suppress them. Security on the southern section of the Pinghan Railway remains strict. (5th dispatch)

Page 4

Leizhou Air Force Bombs Qiong Warship 3

Three Aircraft Bombed the Flying Eagle Warship Twice Yesterday Morning Without Success 4

Qionghai Organizations Wire All Agencies Calling for Ceasefire 5

(Hong Kong) Chen Jitang ordered the Leizhou Air Force to bomb the Flying Eagle warship, docked in Qionghai, twice this morning at 4:00 AM and 6:00 AM, using three aircraft. The bombings were unsuccessful. The Flying Eagle returned fire with anti-aircraft guns, also without success. Various organizations in Qiongzhou (Haikou) wired all provinces and agencies, urging them to call for a ceasefire to preserve the nation's vitality. (5th dispatch)

Six Bombs Thrown at Haikou, Qiongzhou 6

(Hong Kong) According to a dispatch from Qiongzhou, after the aircraft bombed the Flying Eagle warship, they proceeded to Haikou, Qiongzhou, and dropped six bombs, causing considerable damage and casualties. (5th dispatch)

Xiao Focheng Says Resolution Not Difficult 7

(Hong Kong) Xiao Focheng stated: 1. A resolution regarding the fleet is largely achieved; efforts to resolve the land forces are underway and should not pose a problem. 2. Representatives of overseas Filipinos returned to Guangdong to inquire about the political situation. Li Zongren explained that Guangdong and Guangxi would cooperate as always. 3. The Fourth Army Corps decided to change its route and enter Jiangxi to avoid misunderstandings. 4. News has it that Japan will deploy 200,000 troops to invade our inland areas. The Southwest government is discussing responses. (5th dispatch)

Wu Tingyang Appointed to Guizhou Provincial Committee 8

(Hong Kong) The Political Affairs Council decided to appoint Wu Tingyang to the Guizhou Provincial Committee. (5th dispatch)

Peng's Bandits Use All Their Strength 9

To Attack the Guangdong Army Line 10

Attempt To Cut Off the Jiangxi-Guangdong Link Failed 11

(Nanchang) Peng's bandits, fleeing from Yangjiansi on the border of Chongyi and Nankang Counties to Xincheng, launched a full-scale attack on the Guangdong Army's Xinchi defense line in Dayu on the 2nd, attempting to cut off the Jiangxi-Guangdong connection. The Guangdong Army bravely fought back, and another unit flanking the bandits from Chongyi launched a pincer attack, killing over a thousand bandits, seizing six hundred guns. Captured bandits confessed that their pseudo-division commander was also killed. (5th dispatch)

A Portion Attempts a Northern Assault on Lecheng 12

(Nanchang) A telegram from Le'an on the 29th reports that a portion of Peng's bandits fled to Dalu Ping, attempting a northern assault on Lecheng. Hao Menglin's division is currently blocking and suppressing them. (5th dispatch)

Communist Bandits Repelled in Nanxiong 13

(Hong Kong) A telegram from Nanxiong reports that government troops engaged in fierce battles with communist bandits in Zhuji Lane and Xiaoling on the morning of the 3rd. The bandits have been repelled. (5th dispatch)

He Jian Telegram Claims Peace and Security on the Hunan Border 14

(Changsha) He Jian reported to Chiang Kai-shek that Peng's bandits had fled to Xincheng in southern Jiangxi. There are currently no large bandit groups in western Jiangxi. Efforts to eradicate bandits along the Hunan border are underway. He's bandits, due to high waters, were unable to cross south and fled to Hao Cave in Jiangling. The Hunan border is peaceful and secure. (5th dispatch)

Red Bandits Counterattack Shizhong 15

(Xiamen) On the 2nd, the Red bandits counterattacked Shizhong, engaging in fierce battles until the morning of the 3rd, before retreating from Longyan to support Hexi. Frontline contact continues intermittently. The militia withdrew to Longtan Luoping support teams returned to Shizhong for defense, and wired the 49th Division stating, "It is reported that 4,000 Red bandits arrived in Yancheng on the 29th to supply Hexi with one airplane, intending to launch a large-scale counterattack on Shizhong on the 4th and 5th. Our troops lack grain, please provide assistance." (5th dispatch)

Chen Jiliang Arrives in Xiamen on the Hai Chou 16

(Xiamen) Chen Jiliang arrived in Xiamen on the Hai Chou at 1:00 PM on the 5th from Fujian, staying on the ship without disembarking. It is said that he came to resolve the Zhongshan warship issue. (5th dispatch)

Weng Zhaoyuan Leads Troops to Xiamen 17

(Jiangxi) Brigade Commander Weng Zhaoyuan arrived in Jiangxi on the afternoon of the 5th and at 3:00 AM on the morning of the 6th, led the Sixth Regiment aboard the Gongping and Chang'an vessels to Fujian to garrison Xiamen. (5th dispatch)

Fang Zhimin Invades Pan Ting, Pucheng 18

(Fuzhou) A large force of communist bandits under Fang Zhimin invaded Pan Ting, Pucheng, threatening to attack the county seat on the 8th. Liu Heding has taken strict precautions. (4th dispatch)

Zhongda Faculty 19

Continue to Demand Salary from Ministry of Education 20

Zhu Jiahe and Qian Changzhao Both Avoid Meeting 21

Government Has No Funds to Pay Salaries, Creating Impasse 22

(Nanjing) Over thirty representatives of the faculty of Zhongda University arrived at the Ministry of Education at 9:00 AM on the 5th to continue demanding their salaries. However, Zhu Jiahe had gone to the Executive Yuan, and Qian Changzhao, due to severe questioning from a professor yesterday, did not appear. They then went to the Executive Yuan, where Chu Minyi met with them but gave no satisfactory response. Chu stated that the Ministry of Education was the competent authority, and Minister Zhu had come to Nanjing and could still be contacted at the Ministry of Education. The Yuan provided three cars to take the professors back to the ministry in two trips. By noon, the faculty asked ministry staff to buy flatbreads to satisfy their hunger. At 3:00 PM, Qian arrived at the ministry but still did not appear. Zhu also did not come to the ministry. Ministry staff made phone calls everywhere without success. Zhongda faculty insisted that failing to pay off the back salaries was equivalent to not dissolving the university, and remained firm and unyielding. However, paying off the back salaries would require over 400,000 yuan, and the government's credibility was at stake, preventing it from withdrawing the dissolution order or quickly raising the huge sum. Observers believe this matter has reached an impasse. The professors sat in the Ministry of Education for five hours before dispersing. (5th dispatch)

Executive Yuan Persuades Zhu Jiahe to Stay 23

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan instructed Zhu Jiahe, "Your report is acknowledged. On June 29th, the Provisional Meeting of this Yuan addressed the incident of Zhongda students surrounding and beating Acting President Duan Xipeng. A resolution to persuade you to stay was passed, along with a resolution to temporarily dissolve the university pending thorough reorganization. The academic atmosphere has long been unruly. The current government is determined to rectify this, relying entirely on your planning. It is hoped that you will continue to uphold your principles and overcome difficulties. Please do not resign, in order to fulfill our expectations." (5th dispatch)

Duan Xipeng Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday for Medical Treatment 24

(Nanjing) Acting President Duan Xipeng of Zhongda University, after receiving treatment at the Central Hospital, has generally recovered from external injuries. However, his ribs still ache occasionally, and his chest breathing has not returned to normal. He traveled to Shanghai on the evening of the 5th from the Zhongda Hospital to seek renowned doctors for further examination. (5th dispatch)

Receiving Committee Issues Statement 25

(Nanjing) Xie Shuying, Yi Keyi, and Zhou Gan, members of the Ministry of Education's receiving committee for Zhongda University, issued a statement: "We were ordered to handle the handover of Zhongda University. On the 2nd, we received the document and registration departments. On the 3rd, we received the Morning College. On the 4th, we received the general affairs, publishing, and accounting departments, as well as the medical department and library, completing the handover. Personnel were assigned to be responsible for safekeeping and organizing. After the announcement of the verification period, students also began to leave the school. According to reports from dormitory staff, only over 300 students remain. Everything is proceeding smoothly. We were preparing to receive the engineering and science colleges when the heads of the engineering college stated that the colleges could not advance or retreat with the president, and the faculty meeting decided that handover was inconvenient. Furthermore, during the takeover of the library, a faculty member interfered, claiming that our takeover was illegal, intending to obstruct the closure. Given the opinions of the colleges, and to avoid conflict, we should return to the ministry for instructions. However, our handover efforts have reached a small stage. We will await further government orders on how to proceed. This is the past situation of the takeover and the reason why it is temporarily suspended today." (5th dispatch)

Wu Zhihui Dares Not Mediate 26

(Nanjing) Wu Zhihui responded to an interviewer, "I have always been afraid of strangers and dare not mediate. There is no so-called mediation. Everything is fine now and I don't think there will be any further issues. As for refugees, we must also find a place to accommodate them to prevent them from becoming displaced. How much more students? I believe the government will not force them to leave school. As for professors demanding salaries, as the saying goes, 'Ten teachers, nine are poor.' They should be paid for their work, that is our duty. If they don't get paid, they will go home and their wives will want to eat, so how will they manage? As for the separate establishment of educational, literary, and science colleges in Xihan and other places, I really cannot believe it. To cause a student movement, it doesn't matter how many people there are. Three or five people can cause a great disturbance. Therefore, I don't think this is a fundamental solution to eliminating student movements." (5th dispatch)

Principles for Recovering Bandit-Controlled Land 40

Determined in Draft 41

(Nanjing) The issue of recovering land in bandit-controlled areas is difficult to quantify, so several basic principles have been determined in a draft: 1. A committee will be established in the recovered bandit areas to handle land surveying, registration, and distribution. 2. Limits will be set on the maximum and minimum amount of land allocated per person. 3. People who own land can apply for it, but must cultivate it themselves and cannot sublet or sell it. 4. Farmers who own land must pay the government the lowest possible rent, and the government will use the rent revenue to manage local post-disaster reconstruction and provide for the elderly and poor. 5. Temple properties, charitable granaries, school lands, and forests in recovered bandit areas will be taken over for public use for local public welfare. 6. Debt and credit relationships arising from the land will be cancelled. The plan will be implemented after it is passed by the Legislative Yuan. (5th dispatch)

Wharf Company 42

Official-Private Partnership Entanglements 43

(Nanjing) In 1920, the Ministry of Communications and Chen Fuer and others, the founders of the China Wharf Company, entered into an agreement for the joint management of the China Wharf Company. Once the Ministry of Communications recovered the Yangtze Wharf from the Japanese Marine Company, it would be handed over to the company. The official share capital was 180,000 yuan, while Chen Fuer and others were responsible for raising 220,000 yuan as commercial shares, for a total share capital of 400,000 yuan to form a limited liability company. Last July, after the Ministry of Communications sent personnel to recover the wharf from the Japanese Marine Company, the company was supposed to be established according to the contract. The Ministry promptly paid its share according to the agreement. However, Chen Fuer and others from the commercial side repeatedly claimed that the current situation was turbulent and there were changes to the subscribed shares. The Ministry pointed out that two years had passed since the agreement, and the date stipulated in the agreement for the establishment of the company had also passed by five months. The commercial shares had not been fully paid, and there were still many evasions, making it impossible to operate. The Ministry's losses were already considerable and the commercial shareholders should be held responsible for compensation. According to statistics, from July of the 20th year to May of this year, the Ministry had incurred expenses of 8,931 yuan for personnel to guard the wharf, and from July of the 20th year to February of this year, the rent was calculated at 11,200 yuan in silver dollars according to the 7,400 silver dollars per month charged by the Marine Company. Regarding these two items, the Ministry, in accordance with the contract, wired the commercial shareholders to pay the compensation in full within three days. Failure to pay within the deadline would result in the cancellation of the contract and share capital. (5th dispatch)

Luo Gejieff, Director of the Materials Division of the Chinese Eastern Railway, Imprisoned 44

For Misappropriating Railway Funds to Redeem Kidnapped Railway Employees 45

(Harbin) According to a Russian newspaper here, Luo Gejieff, the Director of the Materials Division of the Chinese Eastern Railway Bureau in Hengdaohezi, has been recalled by the Russian authorities and imprisoned in a Russian prison on an island in the White Sea for forcefully demanding railway funds to pay the ransom for kidnapped railway employees. It is said that ten Russian employees of the Chinese Eastern Railway were previously kidnapped, and Luo Gejieff insisted that the Director-General of the Chinese Eastern Railway provide 5,000 yuan in railway funds as ransom. However, the Director-General of the Railway Bureau feared setting a bad precedent and emboldening kidnappers, so he refused. Luo Gejieff reiterated his request, stating that he would forcibly take railway funds to carry out his plan. One day, Luo even drew a pistol and demanded 3,500 yuan from the accountant, combining it with the railway funds he had previously withheld, totaling 5,000 yuan, and redeemed the ten railway employees. Later, it was heard that Luo was recalled to his country, and upon arriving in Russia, he was arrested and imprisoned in the Solovetsky (Solovki) Prison in the White Sea. (5th Reuters)

Foreign Dispatches 77

Lausanne Conference Situation Still Chaotic 78

France Firm That Germany Must Pay 4 Billion Marks in Reparations 79

Italian Representative Suddenly Proposes Total Cancellation of Reparations and War Debts 80

Saying Meeting's Purpose Is To Revive Economy, Not Collect Debts 81

Britain Says It Cannot Yield Further, Declares It Unwilling To Make Further Sacrifices 82

Scheduled To Take Office As Foreign Minister Today 83

▲National News Agency, Lausanne, 4th: The reparations conference has taken a sudden turn today and may reach its peak tomorrow. French Premier Herriot has suddenly decided to return to Lausanne one day early, tonight, as an indication that a resolution is imminent. Today, British Prime Minister MacDonald met with German Premier Papen, followed by a lengthy meeting of representatives from the five creditor nations. However, all negotiations and discussions were held behind closed doors. There is no confirmed news as to how they proceeded tonight. Tonight, British Prime Minister MacDonald also met with representatives from the smaller creditor nations to inform them of the outcome of the negotiations.

▲National News Agency, Lausanne, 4th: Today, Foreign Minister Grandi unexpectedly met with French reporters, forcefully arguing for the necessity of cancelling all reparations. He repeatedly cited the New Testament's maxim of "Forgive and you will be forgiven" as the basis, stating that after three weeks of negotiation at the conference, he was increasingly convinced that the only solution to the situation was to accept the inevitable and totally cancel all reparations and war debts. The Lausanne Conference was not convened to collect future payments. If the purpose is to collect reparations, it will only deepen the current extraordinary situation. The purpose of the conference is to restore confidence and normalcy to the economy, which can only be achieved by canceling all war debts and reparations.

▲National News Agency, Lausanne, 5th: Italian Foreign Minister Grandi reiterated to Associated Press reporters this afternoon that Italy refused to reduce reparations without a corresponding reduction in war debts owed to Britain. He stated that Italy could not sign the five-nation plan or other agreed solutions until it received a guarantee from the British that the war debts owed to Britain could be similarly cancelled or reduced. He was very surprised when British Prime Minister MacDonald handed him the five-nation plan, asking Italy to give up all claims to German reparations, without mentioning Italy's war debts owed to Britain. He also stated that the joint declaration of June 17, which simultaneously suspended payments of reparations and war debts, was the correct way to resolve this issue.

▲National News Agency, Berlin, 5th: At present, German attention to the Lausanne Conference has reached a fever pitch. All speculations and conversations are focused on the developments in Lausanne. Other issues, including the parliamentary elections, have taken a backseat. However, the situation in Lausanne is constantly changing and has become increasingly chaotic recently. The only thing that is clear here is that the conference will be completed within the next 24 or at most 48 hours. The final decision rests entirely with France, especially with French Premier Herriot, who returned to Lausanne this morning.

▲Reuters, Lausanne, 5th: The statements made by the Italian representative last night surprised those attending the reparations conference. There are varying interpretations of these remarks. Some believe they were intended to win American sympathy, while others see them as encouraging German obstinacy. In its statement, Italy expressed regret over the uncertain attitude of European nations towards resolving the issue of war debts. It also stated that the method of total cancellation had been decided on the day the reparations conference opened. It also said that we must be careful not to let the negotiations forget the purpose of this conference. The solution must be a final solution, and the cancellation must apply equally to European countries that are creditors and debtors of reparations or war debts. Foreign Minister Grandi had recently stated to British Prime Minister MacDonald that Italy accepted the British and French proposals but advocated total cancellation. Therefore, this statement may only be a formal gesture. Some sources believe that Italy's statement is tantamount to rejecting the draft agreement.

▲National News Agency, Lausanne, 4th: Italy is deeply displeased with the failure of what it calls the "total cancellation plan." The Italian representative paid a special visit to British Prime Minister MacDonald tonight to inquire about the British position. If Italy's reparations are effectively reduced to nothing, what would the British intend to do with Italy's war debts to Britain? Representatives from each of the invited nations also gathered for an hour this evening to express their dissatisfaction. Representatives from the five inviting nations who drafted the new plan did not

Business and Finance Spot Gold Rises Again by Ten Taels ▲ The General Impression of a Rapid Rise: Yesterday, the price of spot gold rose sharply, giving the general impression of a rapid rise. Very few were selling at the opening. The initial market did not exceed two taels. However, the later market was turbulent, with fluctuations of two to three taels. The overall market fluctuated up and down, exceeding fifteen taels. In the end, there was a sharp rise of ten taels. People were determined to buy. From a slight increase in the morning, it surged to ninety, exceeding the 770 taels mark. Big players bravely bought in, and short sellers rushed to cover, causing a big stimulus. When the silver market stabilized, local drafts tended to firm up. The situation in the later market was chaotic. A new price of 778 taels and 8 mace was seen. Unexpectedly, the drafts were nominally tight but actually stable. Banks suddenly sold U.S. dollars. As a result, various firms on the floor came back to sell. The price then turned down. Finally, it was counted at 73 taels and some odd change. The speed of the change was difficult to fathom. The details of the day are recorded below: ▲ Breaking Out of the 70 Taels Mark: The opening price for August was slightly up by 9 qian, at 764 taels and 3 qian. Large bars were as before. The American silver market was closed. Then it rose again because Wanhsing, Tongchang, and Chunyuhe first started selling, resulting in 65 taels and 2 qian. [H<Fourth Sheet>H[Jinan Steamer Discovers Abduction Case

Relief Society investigators Chen Shaoting and Lin Yongfang recently discovered on the Jinan steamer heading to Xiamen, two abducted women, Xu Guo and Xu Sun, and two abducted boys, eight and four years old. After questioning, it was learned that they were being trafficked from Wuhu to Xiamen for sale. They were immediately detained and handed over to the water patrol police station, and then transferred to the local court. After investigation, prosecution was approved. Yesterday, Judge Guan opened a court session to hear the case. As the case was clear, Xu Guo and Xu Sun were sentenced to one year and two months of imprisonment respectively. The abducted children were sent to the Relief Society for care, pending identification by their families. China Film Art Research Association

▲Compilation and Publication of (Daily Film)

Yan Duhe, Zhou Shoujuan, Pan Gongzhan, Ma Chonggan, Zhu Yingpeng, Yao Sufeng, and others have recently launched the China Film Art Research Association, soliciting supporting members, and compiling and publishing a journal called (Daily Film) every day, starting from the eighth of this month, attached to the Morning Post for distribution. All those who directly subscribe to the Morning Post for the whole year can join the association as supporting members. Information on the origins and membership application methods can be obtained by writing to the Morning Post.

Fire at Tongfu Road

Yesterday at 3:55 PM, a fire broke out in the warehouse on the second floor of Da Zhonghua Foreign Goods Store at 229-235 Tongfu Road, causing smoke and flames to engulf the area. A large number of imported cloth pieces were burned. The fire brigade rushed to the scene upon hearing the alarm and worked hard to extinguish the fire, which was finally put out at 5:00 PM. It is estimated that the loss of goods is about two to three thousand taels. It is reported that the store moved to this location just over a month ago and did not have fire insurance.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce

National Goods Market Continues Low Prices for One Month

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce National Goods Market, since the opening of the National Exhibition, has been holding low prices for one month to thank patrons. It is now reported that yesterday was the end of the low-price period. The Chamber of Commerce, in order to meet the needs of society, has decided to continue the low prices for one month, starting today, requiring participating factories and stores to prepare sufficient summer goods and sell them at wholesale prices to fulfill the purpose of promotion. It is reported that the Chamber of Commerce, in addition to newspaper advertisements, has also asked the Asia-America Wireless Radio Company to broadcast information.

Re-election of Standing Committee of New Pharmaceutical Industry Association

The New Pharmaceutical Industry Association held its first joint meeting of directors and supervisors yesterday (4th). More than ten people, including Chu Minyi and Chen Xingwu, attended. The meeting elected the Standing Committee and Chairman. As a result, Zhang Xianda was elected as Chairman, and Tu Kaizheng, Yuan Hesong, Fan Hefu, and Sun Pingjie were elected as Standing Committee members.

Record of the Qimen Fellow Villagers Association Hosting Tea Merchants Meeting

The Qimen Fellow Villagers Association in Shanghai hosted a banquet for tea merchants at the Daya Restaurant the night before last. More than a hundred tea merchants, including Wang Weiying, Wang Yusan, Xie Buying, Wang Weibin, Kang Dingdong, and Hu Zhifu, attended. Chairman Xu Xiaofu gave a welcome speech, stating that silk and tea were originally major export commodities of our country. In recent years, the silk industry has declined sharply. This year, the tea market has also suffered a setback due to the current situation and financial relations. The root cause is the lack of unity, making it easy to be controlled by others in purchasing and selling, leading to various malpractices. If we do not take immediate action to remedy the situation, we will inevitably become more pessimistic. The Association is willing to work with you to encourage each other. He also reported on the accounts for the 20th year. After discussion, it was decided to strengthen efforts to fight against the special tax levied in Anhui. Regarding the case of Weng Yuanzhen, a pawnshop owner from Qingfu, deliberately killing fellow villager Jiang Zhenfang, the association should forward the family's request for relief to the authorities for speedy arrest and severe punishment of the murderer, and entrust lawyer Xu Kaixian, the legal advisor of the association, to provide legal assistance. All important proposals were discussed and the banquet ended at 9:00 PM.

Hongshun Mutual Aid Association Celebrates Relocation to New Location

The Hongshun Mutual Aid Association held a members' get-together and celebration at its new location in Hongkou yesterday. Guests from various social groups attended, including the Lingnan Tongqun Music and Sports Association lion dance troupe. National arts performances, new dramas, and refreshments were provided to add to the excitement. During the tea party, the chairman spoke, stating that the association's relocation has been completed, and they are honored by the presence of guests from all walks of life. He expressed gratitude for the gifts and pledged to continue the spirit of mutual aid to promote social well-being, seeking guidance from all sectors to benefit the future.

Yin Zhenyi Specializes in Pediatrics

Doctor Yin Zhentian's son, Yin Zhenyi, a doctor at the intersection of Xihoujia Road and Chenghuang Temple, specializes in pediatrics. All kinds of children's miscellaneous diseases can be cured with his prescriptions. Upon the recommendation of a friend, Dr. Yin Zhenyi was consulted, and the condition improved rapidly after taking the medicine, demonstrating Dr. Yin's exquisite medical skills and miraculous effects.

Distribution of Five Weaknesses and Seven Injuries Blood Vomiting Pills

Wang Jun Zhu Yan, from 173 Danfeng Road, Nanshi, this city, his elder brother suffered from hemoptysis for several years. He tried various Chinese and Western medicines, but to no avail. Later, he obtained a prescription from a friend and tried it, which proved effective. This pill specializes in treating five weaknesses and seven injuries, hemoptysis, and other symptoms. However, the cost of the medicine is high, and the poor may not be able to afford it. Wang Jun specially made a grand wish to distribute the pill formula and the pills themselves. The poor can ask for the pills in person, while those who have some financial means can just obtain the formula and make them themselves.

Honor for Physician Chen Cheng

▲Lu Liankui and Others Present a Plaque

Shao Jingfan, a detective at the Old Zha gate police station in the Public Concession, bravely captured a thief on Yunnan Road Yude Lane on April 23, resulting in a gunshot wound to his chest. The bullet penetrated his large intestine, and his condition was critical. He was sent to Renji Hospital by his colleagues and underwent surgery by Dr. Chen Cheng, who provided careful diagnosis and treatment. After being hospitalized for more than two months, he finally recovered. Now, Chief Chinese Detective Lu Liankui and others, recognizing Dr. Chen's profound medical skills, specially made a plaque with the inscription "Miraculous Hands Bring Back Spring" and sent it to Renji Hospital yesterday morning around 11:00 AM with military music. Dr. Chen personally welcomed them and invited them into the living room for a short rest before hanging the plaque indoors. Lu Liankui and others then took their leave. The signatories are Lu Liankui, Liu Shaokui, Feng Zhiming, Tang Jian, Shen Changgen, Cai Yong, and Shao Jingfan.

Cihui Hospital Relocates Back to Original Location

According to the Shanghai Times, Cihui Hospital at 72 Bazilu (Targets Road) was forced to close due to the Japanese invasion of Shanghai, as the hospital was close to the war zone and unable to operate. Furthermore, the hospital's doctors, out of patriotism and love for their hometown, mostly joined the rescue team to provide medical services. Only a small part of the hospital remained, forming a branch hospital on Parker Road, presided over by the hospital director, Cui Wenlan. Now that the war has become a thing of the past and the war zone has mostly returned to normal, the hospital has also relocated back to its original location, renovated and reorganized, looking brand new, and has resumed normal operations. It is said that the hospital's medical services, in addition to internal medicine, surgery, and obstetrics and gynecology, are especially famous for pediatrics.

Mounted Patrol Officer Peel Retires and Returns Home

According to the Shanghai Times, Peel, a mounted patrol officer in the Public Concession police, came to Shanghai in 1910 and has made outstanding contributions to the mounted patrol. He is now retiring due to old age and will return to England with his wife by ship this morning (5th). Colleagues from the police department presented him with a silver tea set yesterday (4th) as a memento.

Publication of the First Issue of the Colonization Monthly

The first issue of the Colonization Monthly, published by the China Colonization Society, was released on July 1st. Key articles include Ma Xiangbo's "Talking about Colonization," Yu Tianxiu's "The Trend of Chinese National Migration and Its Gains and Losses," Zhou Nianxian's "How to Build Border Hydropower Plants," Lü Xinbo's "An Overview of Border Defense," Wang Yang's "The Significance of the Society Convening a National Joint Conference of Colonization Organizations," "A Message to the People of the Country," Ma Junshi's "The General Situation of the Border Regions Before 1932," and other border news and member communications. It is a must-read publication for those concerned about the future of the country and seeking solutions to the entire livelihood issue. The retail price per issue is 2 cents, and the annual subscription for twelve issues, including postage, is 30 cents within the country (same as the domestic price for border provinces). The postage for each issue abroad is an additional 5 cents. A complimentary copy of the first issue will be provided, but a 2-cent stamp must be enclosed for mailing. The publishing office is located at the Society Publication Department of the China Colonization Society, 206 Wenyuanfang, Emory Road, Shanghai. Major bookstores are also selling it.

Establishment of the Social Daily All-Purpose Consulting Agency

The Social Daily recently established the (All-Purpose Consulting Agency) to facilitate inquiries on various social issues from readers in other locations and subscribers in this city. Subscribers can ask and receive answers to all questions. The legal department is staffed by Wu Jingxiong, E Sen, Jiang Yiping, and Wang Peiyuan. The medical department is staffed by Pang Jingzhou, Zhu Shoutian, Ding Zhongying, and Chen Cunren. The fiction department is staffed by Wang Zhongxian, Zhang Chunfan, Qin Shouou, and Zhang Qiuchong. The art and literature department is staffed by Wang Aoxi and Chen Lingxi. The art department is staffed by Ding Su, Zhang Dihan, and Yao Jiguang. The English department is staffed by Zhang Shiliu and Lu Xuehuan. The agency department is staffed by Hu Xiongfei and Chen Huilin. It was officially established the day before yesterday.

Sales of Yue Li Chang E Mosquito Coil

The Yue Li Chang E brand mosquito coil, a well-known product of the Yonghe Industrial Company in this city, has a strong insecticidal effect. Lighting it at night can eliminate mosquitoes, and it is harmless to humans and animals. The price is also very low. It is reported that major stores in this city and other locations are selling it. Those who suffer from mosquitoes at the beginning of summer should have it prepared.

Wuxi fried gluten is traditionally famous, but inconvenient to carry. The Sanle Agricultural Products Society has specially set up a factory in Wuxi to produce it meticulously, making it suitable for cooking and extremely delicious. It is canned and sold to various places. It is especially suitable for vegetarians in the summer and is a good food for families.

Mr. Zhao has been engaged in this industry for more than 20 years and has rich knowledge and experience. His decoration and design are particularly insightful. The store displays various appliances, all of which are the latest styles. Today, they are holding a five-day sale to show preferential treatment and as a commemoration.

The Dalu Cotton Weaving Factory at 739 Elkin Road was founded by Lu Jianqing, the former manager of the Sanxin Company and the business director of the Anlu Cotton Weaving Factory, with funds raised from various sources. It has only been open for three months, but its business is booming. Orders are pouring in from Tianjin, Beiping, Hankou, Guangdong, Hangzhou, and other places. The factory's products are cheap and of good quality, and wholesale prices are especially favorable.

The New World Hotel, located beside the racetrack, has a magnificent building, elegant furnishings, fresh air, and unparalleled coolness. Its location is the best among the hotels in Shanghai. Recently, it has planned to spend the summer by opening the grand hall on Tibet Road as an ice room and opening the rooftop garden. It offers Chinese and Western cuisine, and all kinds of banquets and small drinks are meticulously prepared by famous chefs. Opening a bottle and having a night banquet, cooling off on the top of the building, is truly a scenic spot for spending the summer.

Mr. Pan Zixie has recently collaborated with his fellow student Fang Jiekang on painting a hundred fan leaves to share with friends and to pass the long summer. Mr. Pan draws from the Four Wangs, using a simple and elegant brush, and the colors are ancient and elegant, deeply capturing the charm of harmony and majesty. Mr. Fang is well-versed in epigraphy, and his writings and calligraphy have long been famous in the art world. This move will surely attract many seekers. Collection locations include Lilli Company, Xiling Seal Society, Rong Baozhai, Shanghai Newspaper Office Yin Shoubo, 55 Mingdeli, Foch Road, and other places.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Hindenburg's Annual Salary

Buddha

According to a Berlin dispatch yesterday, Hindenburg's annual salary is less than one-twelfth of that of the presidents of the United States and France. Hindenburg's annual salary was originally 60,000 marks, but since the emergency order to cut official salaries last year, his own annual salary has also been reduced to 37,800 marks. After deducting his income tax, only over 25,000 marks remain, equivalent to about 6,100 yuan. As president, Hindenburg's annual salary is only this amount.

The financial panic in our country is no different from that in Germany, and the salaries of various committee members and ministers, although better, are also limited. Why is the situation of officials being fat and the people being thin, and officials being happy and the people being miserable, so different and special? I once saw a certain minister who, when he was frustrated in Shanghai, had to consider carefully before buying a hat. Now, where does the money for Buick cars and tall foreign houses come from?

In short, the reason for the current situation of officials being fat and the people being thin is, on the one hand, that there are too many officials, and too many non-officials who are close to officials. On the other hand, it is due to extravagance, debauchery, corruption, and abuse of the law, and unlimited exploitation. Such a situation cannot be fully described. I once read two memorials in history that are still unforgettable. I have excerpted them here. I wonder what the officials in charge will think when they read them.

During the reign of Emperor Lizong of the Song Dynasty, Zhu Zeng, a supervisory censor, memorialized: "The territory is shrinking, and taxes are increasing day by day. The number of officials is increasing, and the scale of regulation is expanding. During the Jingde and Qingli eras, the wealth of more than 320 prefectures was used to provide salaries for more than 10,000 officials. Today, the financial resources of more than 100 prefectures are used to support more than 24,000 redundant officials. Border prefectures have branch transfers, while inland areas are in arrears with regular payments. To ease the burden on the people, we must eliminate redundant officials."

Also, during the reign of Emperor Shenzong of the Ming Dynasty, Li Sancai, the governor of Fengyang, memorialized: "The envoys of levy and monopoly are as urgent as fire, and the decrees of extortion are as dense as hairs. Today, a certain mine yields a certain amount of silver, and tomorrow, a certain tax is added. Today, a certain place has a certain tax, and tomorrow, a certain tax is added. In an area of thousands of miles, imperial envoys are everywhere, coupled with rogues and desperadoes, who are like tigers with wings. Cheng Guangxun, a secretary of the Zhongshu, is especially unscrupulous, falsely claiming imperial orders to defraud money, amounting to tens of thousands. Yesterday, Tao Yunming, a transporter, came from Menglai and said that the inner envoys along the way were digging graves to obtain wealth before stopping. The heart of one person is the heart of thousands of people. Your Majesty loves jewels, and the people also love warmth and food. Your Majesty loves ten thousand generations, and the people also love their wives and children. How can Your Majesty want gold to be higher than the Big Dipper, without allowing the people to have a bushel of grain? How can Your Majesty want to be for the sake of his descendants for thousands of years, without allowing the people to have a moment of peace?"

Literary Arts: Accompanying the Two Elders Tong Zhenbao and Changquan on a Rainy Trip to Tazhi'ao, Returning Past Ayuwang Temple (Two Poems)

Hong Jingshan

Since I came to Baotong, the mountain road has been wet for a long time due to rain. The disordered sand is ankle-deep, and the stream is furious and rapid. The sedan carriers are tired, and the bumping is unfamiliar. The two elders indulge in Zen interests, saying that this is suitable for tranquility. The stupa rises above the sky, and the jade table is hidden. When should I bid farewell to worldly disturbances, and my remaining life can be complete? Looking down on the peaks and ridges, tigers crouch and dragons lurk. Who knows the affairs of the world? One valley is truly secluded. Although there are many sorrows, I can freely eat sesame seeds.

The towering Scripture Pavilion, the color of the tiles shines like agate. The painters of the distant inscription wall, their autumn tombs are half-covered with grass. Why should we discuss the Five Mountains? This scenery is naturally good. When did the reclining Buddha begin? It has seen the world and does not age. My interest in viewing is not exhausted, and a hall is being built. Bamboo heads and wood chips, monks can sweep away in the rain. Gradually, I hear the sound of bells, and my happy heart is even more overturned. Why suppress disordered thoughts? I entrust everything to nothingness. There are dragons and elephants in the Buddhist gate. Who will prove the Way?

Science: How to Make Paint

Chao

Paint, its use is also very great. Applied to wooden objects, it can prevent corrosion. Applied to metal objects, it prevents oxidation and rusting, and it can increase beauty.

Paint is divided into two types: Chinese paint and foreign paint. Chinese paint lacks gloss and is cheaper. Foreign paint is more expensive but has gloss. Because it is loved for its gloss, many people prefer to use foreign paint.

Our country's paint is mostly based on tung oil. Tung oil is divided into two types: bright and transparent is called white oil, and black is called black oil. White oil is mixed with white lead powder to make white paint. Approximately five parts of white oil are mixed with three parts of white lead powder. First, add a little kerosene to the lead powder, grind it finely, and sieve it. Then, put it into the white oil and mix evenly to make white paint. To make paints of various colors, just add color to it. However, the color powder must be very fine. To apply it, first use pig blood mixed with a little lime milk, apply it to the wooden object, and after it dries, rub it with grass until it is bright. Then, apply this paint. Usually, it is not applied evenly the first time, so you can apply it twice. Too many times, it is easy to crack.

How to Make Foreign Paint

How to make the bottom layer of paint. Take twenty parts of boiled linseed oil, fifteen parts of pure white lead powder, three parts of fine lead red powder, and fifteen parts of boric acid desiccant. (How to make boric acid desiccant: take one pound of raw linseed oil, one pound of zinc carbonate, and one pound of manganese borate, mix them thoroughly, store them, and use them to make the paint dry easily on the object.) First, mix the lead red and lead powder, sieve them, and add the desiccant and linseed oil. Be sure to mix it evenly. Then, you can use a brush to apply it to the wooden object as the bottom layer of paint. You should brush it thinly and evenly. On top of the bottom layer, you should brush a layer of glossy paint to make it brighter. Take fifteen parts of fine white lead powder, ten parts of raw linseed oil, seven parts of desiccant, ten parts of turpentine oil, and twenty parts of boiled linseed oil. First, mix the lead powder with the raw and boiled linseed oil, then add the desiccant, mix, and then add the turpentine oil and mix evenly to make the paint. If the paint is thick, you can add turpentine oil to mix it. After brushing, the brush should be placed in turpentine oil; otherwise, it will be difficult to wash when it dries.

Problem Office: The Vase in the Office

Zhu

In the past, when I was in school, I skipped class two out of three days, and Miss Zhang, who took the "shortcut" as her motto, actually managed to get a high school diploma last summer. As for her aspirations, she originally wanted to go to university and study further; however, her father failed in speculative business, and her finances did not allow it, thus arousing her determination to seek a career.

In addition to widely entrusting relatives and friends to introduce her to a suitable position, she paid attention to job advertisements in the newspaper every day.

One day, she saw such an advertisement posted by a large institution:

"A certain institution needs several female secretaries, who must be young and have a pretty face, and have a high school diploma. Those who are willing to apply should submit a detailed resume, along with a half-length photo, to PO Box XX. Those who are qualified will be invited for an interview. Those who are not qualified will not be replied to."

She busily wrote an application letter, attached a recent small photo of herself dressed in fashionable clothes, and sent it solemnly by registered mail.

She eagerly waited until the sixth day before she received a reply letter inviting her for an interview. Knowing that there were some hopes, she happily prepared to go for the interview.

Therefore, she first went to the barber shop to perm her hair, put on lipstick, and deliberately put on makeup, and then changed into a new cheongsam and walked towards the recruiting institution.

From afar, she saw a simply dressed woman in cloth, whom she recognized as Miss Wang, a classmate who was known as the "top female scholar." She hurried up to greet her: "Wang, are you also here for the interview? With your talent in writing and calligraphy, I am sure to fail."

Miss Wang, although modest, was confident that "with my usual academic ability, I should be able to fill the position of a writing secretary."

Unexpectedly, the result of the interview was beyond her expectations. Miss Wang failed, while Miss Zhang was hired.

When Miss Zhang received the notice of acceptance, she secretly felt ashamed, because when she returned from the interview that day, she remembered that she had mistakenly written "不寒而栗" (bù hán ér lì, shivering with cold) as "而慄" (ér lì) and "永矢勿諼" (yǒng shǐ wù xuān, never forget) as "勿緩" (wù huǎn). She thought she would definitely be rejected and had no hope. Now, she was actually loved by the examiner and hired. This was truly a pleasant surprise!

From the next day, she dressed up in fancy clothes every day and went to the writing room, sometimes not returning until late at night. When asked what kind of official business she was so busy with, she could not say why.

Some people say that Miss Zhang's job in the office is very leisurely, just like a vase with fresh flowers, pleasing the director, a flower that understands words and exudes fragrance!

Doing Business at the Pawnshop

Rong Ping

A difficult life often makes me go in and out of the doors of the "pawn" shop. But not because it is "often," I feel uneasy when I walk in.

Last night, I walked with a friend again. Entering the iron gate, passing through the screen with the big character "(pawn)," as usual, I saw two or three arrogant shop assistants standing on the high counter. When they saw you coming in, they would not even greet you. At this moment, I am afraid that everyone will sigh and say: "(The pawnshop) door is as deep as the sea!"

I respectfully handed the package up with both hands and stood there blankly waiting, my hopeful eyes fixed on the shop assistant who was opening my package and examining it. I also felt a little pitiful. And he, all he did was nag and complain. The distance was too high, so I couldn't hear clearly, but anyone who has experience with this transaction knows that he is there to find fault with your things and say that they are worthless.

"(How much do you want to pawn it for?)" he asked after a minute.

"(How much are you willing to offer?)"

"(Four dollars)"

"(Too little! Do you want eight dollars?)"

"(No, four and a half dollars at most.)"

"(We want to redeem it, exactly six dollars······)"

Before I could finish speaking, he had already pushed the package to the edge of the counter. If you don't rush to pick it up, he will unceremoniously push it down. Needless to say, he is unwilling to pack it for you with his noble hands.

I ran to the second one, and all the situations were mostly the same. When the shop assistant, perched high on the counter, arrogantly threw the question "(How much do you want to pawn it for?)," I replied: "(Seven dollars)" (The lesson from the previous one made me lower the price by one dollar myself.) Even worse! He offered one dollar less than the previous one! Three dollars. I was a little annoyed at this time. But the arrogant voices of these gentlemen are ultimately unbearable. Going to the third one, wouldn't the same arrogant faces be waiting for you there? Who would be willing to look at so many faces and get half a dollar more, let alone be sure that it would be less than here. In the end, it took a lot of talking to complete the transaction for four dollars. Holding the four dollars and the pawn ticket and walking out of the solemn gate, I felt much more relaxed all over, because I had finally completed a troublesome negotiation.

Little Secrets: Experience Riding the Tram

Wang Chaoran

I travel dozens of miles every day, and the tram fare is a huge expense, so I have a lot of experience riding the tram. Now I will write a little bit below, which may be helpful for some people.

(1) On the tram, it is best not to sit close to people who smoke cigarettes: otherwise, when a gust of wind comes, the thick smoke will blow in your face, easily causing you to cough and shed tears. The cigarette ash will fly around, blowing on your body like stars twinkling and sparks flying, often burning your hands or clothes and burning a cigarette hole.

(2) On a long-distance trolley bus, if you are afraid of getting dizzy from the bumps, it is best to sit near the driving area, or sit in a seat directly above the wheels, which will be less bumpy.

(3) When you get on the tram, if there are no seats available, then start paying attention to the sitting passengers. Whoever has the fewest copper coins in their hand, or who has bought the fewest tickets, you should wait next to him, because he will be getting off soon.

(4) In hot weather, if there are no seats available when you get on the bus, you can wait next to women or children, because when they leave their seats and you sit down, although the seat is very hot, it is extremely difficult to catch venereal diseases.

(5) On the tram, it is best not to sit in a place where the window is open; otherwise, your hat will often disappear without a trace, especially at Dongxin Bridge, you should be especially vigilant.

(6) It is dangerous to walk on Avenue Edward VII, but no matter which tram you take, it is free to pass through Avenue Edward VII. For example, if you take Tram Route 5 to Dongxin Bridge, you can pass through Avenue Edward VII to get off at the vegetable market road.

(7) If you get on and off the tram at a small stop, you will suffer a lot. The tram company has route and price lists for each route. You can write to them to ask for one and read it. Then you will not suffer when you take the tram in the future.

(8) Trolley buses seem to be cheaper and faster than trams, but this is not the case. Therefore, if you are going to a certain place, if there is a tram to take, you would rather walk a few steps more and take the tram. It is more economical in terms of time and money, and it is also more comfortable for your body and mind.

(9) If the tram is very crowded, and someone pretends to be especially squeezed and mutters a lot in their mouth, no matter how beautiful their clothes are or how upper-class their tone is, you must pay attention to your pocket, especially when getting off the bus, you should be extra careful; otherwise, three or four of them will gang up on you, circle you like a robbery, and take your wallet.

Why? A Child's Question

Xing

In the evening, I took my son A Gang for a walk on the road. A red van drove from afar. When it reached the entrance of a lane, it stopped, and several burly men jumped out of the car, searching around with fierce dog-like eyes. Then, two thin, haggard people—no, (beggars)—were grabbed by their tattered clothes like an eagle catching a chicken and thrown into the prison car. Of course, in order to maintain the (order) and (dignity) of this society, it is not permissible to have (freedom to walk) and (freedom to beg).

The red prison car full of (hunger) and (poverty) left. My son A Gang asked me:

"(Why does a good person become a beggar?)"

"(Because they have no food to eat)," I answered him lazily.

"(Why don't they have food to eat?)"

"(Because they don't work!)"

"(Why don't they work? Is it because they don't want to work themselves? Or does society not give them work?······ Moreover, I only see the young master Zhang and the young mistress Zhang next door playing mahjong, watching movies, and dancing every day. I have not seen them work. Why do they have tall foreign houses to live in, gorgeous clothes to wear, cars to ride in, and male servants and female maids to serve them?)"

"(That's because their (fate) is good!)"

"(What is (fate) then? Does fate predetermine that a group of people are born to enjoy happiness, while another large group of people are born to starve, suffer from cold, and be caught and sent to the red prison car?······ Moreover, where do young master Zhang's foreign house, car, and gorgeous clothes come from? Did (fate) send them to him? I did not see it. What is (fate) anyway!)"

Before the child waited for my answer, he continued to ask:

"(Is the prison car catching (beggars)? Or is it catching (hunger)? Can (hunger) be caught? Can (beggars) be caught completely?)"

After the child finished speaking, his eyes fixed on me, waiting for my answer. However, how could I answer? I felt anxious and ashamed in my heart, but I lazily said in my mouth "(Silly child, don't just say silly things!)"

Taking the child home, I thought silently: "(Child, you are great, your doubts are great, and your era will be great!)"

Playing a Trick: Cleverly Devising a Plan to Punish the Shop Assistant

Yi Yi

▲Punishing an Arrogant and Rude Shop Assistant

The day before yesterday, after lunch, during the break, I chatted with a few friends and talked about the arrogant and rude treatment of customers by shop assistants in our country's stores. At that time, I heard what Mr. Zhang said at the meeting, that he had suffered some hardships from a grocery store shop assistant, and everyone applauded.

Mr. Zhang said: "(I remember once, in a grocery store on Nanjing Road, I wanted to buy some dried bamboo shoots. At that time, it was noon, and the shop assistants were eating. I had to wait. After about half an hour, I saw one of the shop assistants finish eating. I said to him, (I want to buy some dried bamboo shoots,) how could I know that he not only ignored me, but did not even look at me, and went straight to wash his face inside. At the time, I thought maybe he didn't hear me. Then I thought that he had just finished eating, with an oily mouth and face, how could he not wash his face and do business, I thought, and my anger subsided. I had to wait again.

After about another ten minutes, the shop assistant came out after washing his face. At this time, I had already gained my first experience. I was afraid that he still wouldn't hear me, so I said a little louder and asked him:

(Do you have any good dried bamboo shoots here?)

Who knew that he only looked at me, walked to the counter with a full air, picked up a water pipe, lit a piece of paper, and leisurely smoked his water pipe.

At this time, I was angry, thinking that this thing was too arrogant and rude to customers. If I didn't think of a way to punish him, how could I get rid of the hatred in my heart? So, a flash of inspiration came, and I actually came up with a clever plan. I still waited patiently for a while, and the shop assistant came out again. I didn't speak at the time, watching what tricks he had. It was ridiculous, he came to ask me, (What do you want to buy?)

So, I said to him, (I want to buy five catties of the best dried bamboo shoots, five catties of white sugar; five catties of brown sugar; three catties of red dates; two catties of black dates; two catties of walnuts; one catty of longans; one catty of lotus seeds; all the best,)

When he heard that I wanted to buy so many things, he thought that I was buying goods for someone, a large business coming to the door, how could he be so slow again

Private Thoughts on Reforming Education Bin. 84

In recent times, insightful individuals within the country are alarmed by the surging tide of student unrest, which grows increasingly fierce. Illiteracy is widespread across the nation, and the number of out-of-school youth and children continues to rise dramatically. Education is deteriorating rapidly, nearing a state of decadence and bankruptcy, a tragic scenario. The nation's future holds hidden crises. Consequently, calls for educational reform are emerging at the opportune moment. A month ago, Chen Guofu of the Central Committee proposed a "Preliminary Plan for Educational Reform," believing that future educational programs should be revised to cultivate individuals with applicable skills to cope with this extraordinary environment. He advocated for universities to focus solely on agriculture, engineering, and medicine; secondary schools to emphasize mathematics, physics, and chemistry; and primary schools to concentrate on Chinese language and arithmetic, to realize "technical education" and "practical education." Subsequently, a respected elder in the education sector, Mr. So-and-so, argued that future education should be "creative education," followed by "technical education." He stated, "There must first be a societal need, and then such education should be established, so that learning and application can align." Even the media has put forward various reform proposals to salvage our nation from this great crisis. Amidst the nationwide chaos of pursuing only profit and vying only for power, the fact that some still pay attention to the educational issue, which is deeply connected to the nation's destiny, is indeed a somewhat gratifying phenomenon. However, this matter is of utmost importance, and reform is not easily achieved. It requires insightful individuals from across the nation to come together for discussions and pool their wisdom to hopefully find a good remedy to revive this decadent and bankrupt education. We also wish to express our humble opinions and offer them as suggestions.

Before presenting our reform proposals, we must first examine the current state of decadence in our nation's education. We are not intentionally exposing ugliness, but the reality is that today's education is already on the verge of collapse. If we continue to be indifferent, it will ultimately be beyond saving. Only the brave can acknowledge the facts, and only the brave can seek a path to survival from the facts. Our intention is to recognize and grasp the current state of decay and then explore a clear path toward "reform."

Does our nation truly have education to speak of today? Hardly anyone dares to answer definitively. In terms of educational direction, there is no direction to speak of. In terms of educational funding, it is chronically in arrears. The government sees education as a tool for window dressing, and society sees it as a superfluous entity that only breeds negative consequences. Those who are distant lament, while those who are close are even more indifferent and unconcerned. Many of those in the education sector are forced to act due to the pressure of making a living or are trapped by the evil forces of politics. Some even masquerade as educators, vying for positions in education as a stepping stone to obtaining official posts. As a result, primary school education is declining daily, and there is no hope of promoting compulsory education. The number of illiterate adults cannot be reduced gradually, and more and more youth and children are being pushed into the ranks of the illiterate. The impoverished countryside is, of course, a given. Even urban children's education lacks a clear direction and funding. In the arms of ignorant nannies, next to stalls of martial arts and fantastical books, children's education is virtually on its last breath. Then there's secondary school, which should have its own independence, with its purpose not only to prepare students for university but also to cultivate healthy citizens who can live independently. However, today's secondary schools in our country are largely isolated from the practical realities of society. Students' futures are not considered. The creation of unhealthy citizens is not accounted for. Instead of guiding students to integrate with the practical realities of society, they are pulled out of society and put on a path of empty pride, extravagant hopes, incompetence, and uselessness. This is the phenomenon in secondary education that most needs to be reformed. As for university education, it is even more heartbreaking to discuss. Universities have become arenas for political contests, and students are used as expendable tools. Heavy responsibilities in education do not seek specialized talent but only ask about political factions. When one faction rises, another vies for its place. Student unrest arises as a result. Once student unrest starts, there is no way to quell it, so political power is used to suppress it. As for the students themselves, most of them only know arrogance and extravagance, only know how to use university to decorate their appearance and to hunt for fame and fortune. Why study, and how to use what they learn, is not considered. Indulging in song and dance becomes the norm. Those who truly devote themselves to their studies are derided as bookworms. Even if they are successful in their studies, society cannot use them. Even worse, the higher the level of education, the more obvious the monopoly becomes. Secondary school requires one to two hundred gold pieces a year, which is beyond the reach of children from middle-class families and below. As for university, the children of the impoverished are left only with a sigh of despair. This type of monopolistic, aristocratic education, wanting to seek its development, wanting to lay the new foundation of our nation, is even more impossible.

In short, our nation's education today has no direction and no plan. Education is hijacked by bureaucracy, used only as a practice ground for political struggles, and only as a furnace for casting high-level vagrants. Therefore, if we do not resolutely reform it today, the crisis will materialize, and the demise of our nation will truly not have to wait ten years.

Domestic Important Telegrams

Jilin Self-Defense Army Plans to Take Changchun 85

Feng Zhanhai as Commander-in-Chief, Gong Changhai as Deputy

Feng's Troops Plan to Counterattack the Japanese Army in Xinlitun

Two Armies Adopt a Coordinated Advancing Style 86

The Jilin Self-Defense Army in Heihe, with Feng Zhanhai as commander-in-chief and Gong Changhai as deputy commander, plans to capture Changchun. The main force of Feng Zhanhai's army is currently concentrated in Tuqiaozi, 23 li east of Xinlitun in Yushu, and plans to counterattack the Japanese army garrison in Xinlitun. Feng's army is currently facing the Murai-Funabashi unit of the Japanese army. Gong Changhai leads more than 2,000 Jilin Self-Defense Army soldiers, concentrated in Sihecheng between Wuchang and Yushu, and adopts a coordinated advancing style with Feng's army's Yao Chengqian and Zhao Wenbin brigades, moving towards Changchun. Sihecheng is 45 li east of Yushu, a strategic location between Wu and Yu. (4th Dispatch)

Ren, the adjutant to the commander of the Japanese army's Okawa Company, who was captured by Feng Zhanhai's army in Heihe, escaped on the 2nd. According to him, Feng Zhanhai's army was previously assembled in Guojiatun, south of Wuchang. The leaders of the Jilin Self-Defense Army in the vicinity of Wuchang are Feng Zhanhai, Gong Changhai, and Yao Chengqian. They will wait for the troops to finish assembling before attacking Yushu, first taking Fangshutun in the southeast as a base. Feng Zhanhai's 700 cavalry are currently active along the Lalin River, watching for opportunities to strike against the Japanese army and the puppet Jilin army. Feng sent a certain staff officer to Beiping to meet with Zhang Xueliang. (4th Dispatch)

Zhang Haipeng's Troops Open Tao Lai Zhao 87

Heihe Zhang Haipeng's army's 6th detachment opened the Tao Lai Zhao on the Ha Chang Line on the evening of the 2nd, defending against the Self-Defense Army. (4th Dispatch)

Fierce Battle Between Japanese Cavalry and Ma's Army 88

Heihe On the 1st, a Japanese army cavalry unit advancing north towards Hailun encountered 700 soldiers of the Ma's army's independent cavalry battalion near Tongbei. They fought fiercely for a long time, and the Jilin Self-Defense Army retreated. (4th Dispatch)

Heihe On the 1st, the Japanese army encountered the elite independent cavalry battalion under Ma Tianlong's command near Huangjiadian, 45 li north of Tongbei. They fought fiercely for a day and a night. Ma's army stood firm and did not retreat. By the afternoon of the 2nd, they retreated in an easterly direction. (4th Dispatch)

Self-Defense Army Gathers North of Jilin 89

(Harbin) According to Japanese aircraft reconnaissance reports, the "Anti-Manchu Army" is currently concentrated eighty miles north of Jilin City, apparently intending to attack Jilin City. Jilin is the terminus of the Jilin-Changchun Railway, approximately sixty miles from Changchun. If the "Anti-Manchu Army" actually attacks, the Japanese will utilize the Jilin-Changchun Railway to deploy a large number of troops for defense, and fierce battles are inevitable. The situation in the eastern section of the Chinese Eastern Railway remains unstable. The Japanese and the "Manchu Puppet State" authorities are trying to restore traffic between Harbin and Suifenhe. Several railway bridges on the Chinese Eastern Railway were blown up by the Anti-Manchu Army on the 1st of this month and are currently under repair. Heavy fighting is expected to break out recently in the Tongbei area north of Hailun. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

Beizhen Righteous Army Attacks Qingduizi 90

(Beiping) Over four hundred righteous soldiers from Beizhen County, in conjunction with more than two hundred members of the Heishan Militia, attacked sixty Japanese soldiers at the Qingduizi Railway Station on the evening of the 2nd. They fought fiercely for a long time. The righteous army once occupied Qingduizi Railway Station, and traffic on the line was stopped for four hours. Later, a large number of Japanese troops arrived, and the righteous army temporarily retreated. (5th Dispatch)

Self-Defense Army Annihilates Enemy in Tonghua 91

(Beiping) The Tonghua Self-Defense Army annihilated the enemy in a night attack some days ago. The enemy suffered extremely heavy losses, and they are currently planning to pursue them north. (5th Dispatch)

The Investigation Team Will Express to Japan 92

Urging them Not to Recognize the Puppet State

Acts of Infringing on Territorial Sovereignty

Are Detrimental to International Standing

(Tokyo) The Japanese government intends to take measures to de facto recognize the independence of "Manchukuo." However, the observation of the investigation team is: (1) Japan's recognition of "Manchukuo" contradicts the former government's statements to the League of Nations regarding respect for Chinese territorial sovereignty, which will be opposed by world opinion. (2) The Japanese government's act is equivalent to recognizing the infringement of territorial sovereignty, which violates the Nine-Power Treaty. Therefore, Japan's recognition of "Manchukuo" is detrimental to Japan's international standing. Furthermore, it will be advised against immediately recognizing "Manchukuo" during the meeting between Count Uchida and the investigation team. As a member of a certain country has already expressed unofficial intentions, the investigation team's actions are highly valued. (5th Domei News Agency Dispatch)

Lytton Recuperating at the British Embassy 93

(Tokyo) Lord Lytton is ill. He was examined by a doctor from the French Embassy. His condition is not serious, but he is suffering from excessive fatigue, and his kidneys are slightly affected, so he needs to rest for two or three days. He is currently recuperating at the American Embassy. His meeting with Prime Minister Saito today has been postponed. (5th Domei News Agency Dispatch)

Secretary-General Haas's Statement 94

(Tokyo) The Secretary-General of the International Investigation Team, Haas, told the press corps last night that he personally is optimistic about the Manchurian issue. The investigation team will only report to the council based on the results of its investigation of the facts. The council, in accordance with Article 15 of the League Covenant, can transfer this report to the League Assembly. (5th Domei News Agency Dispatch)

Meeting with Japanese Prime Minister Today 95

(Tokyo) Due to Lord Lytton's illness from the long journey, the investigation team's meeting with Prime Minister Saito has been postponed until 2:00 PM tomorrow. (5th Domei News Agency Dispatch)

The Extramural Section of the Beining Railway 96

Righteous Army Attacks Train

Japanese Deputy Chief of Staff Masaki Nearly Suffers Misfortune

(Shenyang) While on his way back to Shenyang after inspecting Jinzhou, Deputy Chief of Staff Masaki and his party encountered an incident at 0:50 PM yesterday, between Yangzhangzi and Goubangzi. The leading Japanese armored car was overturned by the Righteous Army, and the Righteous Army, who had been hiding nearby, opened fire fiercely on Masaki's train. The security force telegraphed the Goubangzi garrison for reinforcements, and only then were the Righteous Army driven back. The party arrived in Shenyang at 9:00 PM last night. (5th Domei News Agency Dispatch)

(Tokyo) Japanese Deputy Chief of Staff Masaki is currently inspecting the three eastern provinces. It is reported that he nearly suffered misfortune on the way from Jinzhou to Shenyang yesterday. According to Japanese sources, near Shishan Station, bandits destroyed the tracks, and the armored car escorting Masaki's train derailed. Fortunately, it was not damaged or overturned. Three hundred bandits were not far away, and the armored car immediately opened fire, killing ten bandits. The rest scattered. Masaki continued onward and arrived safely in Shenyang last night. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

Chiang Inspects the Headquarters 97

Meets with Officers Above Battalion Commander

Addresses Focus on Military Discipline

Strictly Prohibiting On-the-Spot Levies

Capital Punishment for Amounts Over 500 Yuan

(Hankou) Chiang Kai-shek met with officers above battalion commander level of the 13th Division at the headquarters on the morning of the 5th and addressed them, mainly focusing on three points: (1) Rectifying military discipline, enhancing the personality of military personnel, and enriching the effectiveness of the army; (2) Not engaging in on-the-spot levies and protecting the local people; (3) Sincerely cooperating with the people. He then met with Peng Zhenshan and scheduled to meet with officers of the 89th Division at the headquarters on the morning of the 6th. Starting from the 7th, he will meet separately with the 88th Division, 83rd Division, Garrison Brigade, and directly subordinate units of the 10th Army on a daily basis. (5th Dispatch)

Chiang Promulgates Regulations on the Punishment of Levy-Raising for Supplies 98

(Hankou) Chiang promulgated the regulations on the punishment of levy-raising for supplies on the 5th: Demotion for 100 Yuan, Removal from office for above 100 Yuan, Capital punishment for above 500 Yuan. He also ordered the Pacification Commissioner's Office to transfer to all agencies that if employees are transferred, they must not be assigned additional responsibilities or arbitrarily increase salaries. (5th Dispatch)

Personnel from the Political Training Department Will Arrive in Hankou Soon 99

(Hankou) He Zhonghan will lead two hundred personnel from the Political Training Department to Hankou on the 6th, where they will be dispatched to various divisions to establish branch offices. (5th Dispatch)

Zhang Qun Has Been Visiting Chiang Repeatedly 100

(Hankou) Zhang Qun visited Chiang at the Yihe residence on the evening of the 4th and the morning of the 5th, and there were consultations. (5th Dispatch)

Hubei Pacification Commissioner's Office Telegraphed to Inquire About Zhang's Departure Date 101

(Hankou) Zhang Juliang plans to come to Hankou to meet with Chiang within the next few days. The Pacification Commissioner's Office has telegraphed Ping, inquiring about the departure date in order to welcome him. (5th Dispatch)

Huang Luchu Will Return to Shanxi After Completing Official Business 102

(Hankou) Xu Yongchang, representing Huang Luchu, has completed his official business in Hankou after meeting with Chiang, and is scheduled to return to Shanxi on the 7th to report back. It is rumored that Chiang has a letter for Xu, which Huang will take with him. (5th Dispatch)

Li Jihong Arrives in Hankou to Meet with Chiang and He 103

(Hankou) Li Jihong arrived in Hankou on the 5th and met separately with Chiang and He. (5th Dispatch)

Yang Hucheng Sends Representative to Hankou 104

(Hankou) Yang Hucheng's representative, Hu Yimin, arrived in Hankou on the 5th to meet with Chiang and visited various military and political authorities for negotiations. (5th Dispatch)

County Magistrates of Various Counties Summoned to Leave the Province 105

(Hankou) County magistrates of various counties have been summoned to come to the provincial capital for a conference and to meet with Chiang for instructions. They are to arrive before the 10th of the month. The provincial government dispatched Section Chief Jiang Wenbo and others on the 5th to receive them. (5th Dispatch)
